That nanny is also my boyfriend.  ||| Cette nanny est aussi mon ami. 
The nanny moved here from Ethiopia where he is from.  ||| Le nanny s'est déplacé ici de l'Éthiopie où il est. 
The nanny arrives early for his shift.  ||| Le nanny arrive tôt pour son changement. 
That nanny is hella strict, watch out for him.  ||| Ce nanny est hella strict, regarde pour lui. 
That nanny retired early, good for him.  ||| Ce nanny se retire tôt, bon pour lui. 
He enjoys his work as a nanny.  ||| Il aime son travail en tant que nanny. 
Though he argued with his colleagues, the nanny was always respectful.  ||| Même s’il a discuté avec ses collègues, le nanny était toujours respectueux.

His brother is a nanny.  ||| Son frère est un nanny. 
His boyfriend is a nanny.  ||| Son petit ami est un nanny. 
The nanny works hard and he excels!  ||| Le nanny travaille dur et il excelle!

My brother enjoys his work as a nanny.  ||| Mon frère jouit de son travail en tant que nanny. 
My boyfriend enjoys his work as a nanny.  ||| Mon copain aime son travail en tant que nanny. 
As a nanny, he is very competent.  ||| En tant que nanny, il est très compétent. 
I talked to him, he is a nanny.  ||| Je lui ai parlé, il est un nanny. 
He works as a nanny.  ||| Il travaille comme un nanny. 
I worked with him, he is a very qualified nanny.  ||| J'ai travaillé avec lui, il est un nanny très qualifié.

That nanny retired early, good for him.  ||| Ce nanny est retraité tôt, bon pour lui. 
He enjoys his work as a nanny.  ||| Il jouit de son travail en tant que nanny.
